Execute Python code in an IPython sandbox and return the output.

The code runs as an **IPython cell** — **NEVER** wrap it in main function.
Inside the sandbox, `call_tool(name, **kwargs)` is *ALREADY* available as a synchronous built-in for registered host callbacks. Use the tool name as the first argument and keyword arguments only — do not pass a dict or any other positional arguments after the tool name.

Prefer `run_python_code` when you need to combine one or more`call_tool(...)` calls with Python control flow, loops, orpost-processing.

Registered sandbox tools:

    Input schema: no input parameters
    Output schema: {'properties': {'apps': {'description': 'List of available apps', 'items': {'properties': {'name': {'description': 'App name', 'title': 'Name', 'type': 'string'}, 'description': {'description': 'Short description of what the app does', 'title': 'Description', 'type': 'string'}}, 'required': ['name', 'description'], 'title': 'AppDescription', 'type': 'object'}, 'title': 'Apps', 'type': 'array'}}, 'required': ['apps'], 'type': 'object'}
